##

2018-01-12 21:51:17
Kuntal Ganguly
32052148
4.5
Ambiance (3.5/5): The place is well known to people who are regular to, or often visit the College Street area. The outlet is more of a shop selling flavored beverages. It is not very spacious and sparsely decorated, but yet is comfortable and a nice place to hangout with mates while sipping on cool, refreshing drinks.

Service/Quality (4.5/5): There isn't anything ornamental about this place, and the staff just come over, take the orders and then shout out the orders to the people in the back. Once ready, the drinks are served at their respective table.¬†Whether it is a hot summer afternoon or a mildly cold evening during winter, the drinks served here are always a delight. It is more about the pleasure than the quality.

Revisit/Recommend (4.5/5): The outlet has been open for a long time, but is still on the top of it's game. Over the years, I have been to this place numerous times with both friends and family, and have never left disappointed or dissatisfied. It is definitely recommended to everyone for a fairly good time.

There are few places left in the city, which will help you explore 'Calcutta', a city which grew with passion and love for aesthetics. Paramount, with its rich neighbourhood of the legendary 'boipara', the educational hubs and the populace who are lovers of art and recluse living is a true testimony to 'simple living & high thinking'. Once you step inside this age old place, you will realize beverages made of passion do not require advertising to attract people from far across the city and beyond. The show stealer - Daber sherbat and other juices are 100% unadulterated. The ambience is quiet with a silent homage to distinguished people who visited Paramount in its 100 year long journey!

Paramount is not a sherbet place its an institution. Beside Indian Coffee House and Dilkhusha Cafe this place is also a legendary place in College street area and it can easily boast for one of the longest serving sherbet place in India. I would recommend this place to everyone who is visiting Kolkata as without visiting this place their trip to kolkata will remain incomplete

2017-09-16 12:05:31
Oishik Sarkar
3119605
4.0
Paramount is a very popular place of North Kolkata located near to College Square. There's hardly someone living in Kolkata, who haven't tried their Sherbats or doesn't know about this place. They're famous for their sherbats & syrups from years that is still maintaining a brilliant quality for respective price.

Paramount is a very basic place that remainds the old culture & looks of Kolkata. Sitting over here looking at the old photo frames with their drinks is refreshing experiance.

One of their most famous drinks are Dub Sarbat & Kesar Malai. Dab Sarbat costs Rs.50 and Kesar Malai was bit expensive at Rs.100.

Dub Sarbat : It wasn't just coconut water, it was something special that was made with experiance from a reputated place. Its sweetness melts the heart while quenching your thirst with the flavour of Coconut. You will see every table have ordered one of this because it's an absolute recommend drink here.

Kesar Malai : It isn't a thick drink like other places rather it was completely lite. Layers of malai & raisins in the drink was the main ingredients making the drink delightful. It tasted totally different than any place & maybe that is their signature.

Paramount is a charm of North Kolkata and a sweet cheers over here is a must.

Paramount is a sherbat and syrup house in College Street, no less than a heritage point now. It mostly remains crowded with college students.
I've visited here so many times for their Dub sherbat. Dub sherbat is chilled coconut water drink with a mild rose water flavor served with a coconut pulp. It's the healthiest option one can choose to beat the heat. It is delicious and that too at an affordable price.
Other than Dub sherbat, I've tried their Cream Kesar Lassi and Strawberry syrup. They are equally delightful and refreshing.
Bangaliyana at its best. Highly recommended. üòä

##

2017-07-15 21:59:34
Subhasish Das
2646
4.0
Paramount does not need any introduction. It is one of the legendary sherbet shop in Kolkata with a lot of heritage attached to it. They are famous for serving eclectic mix of syrups/serbats and special drinks at rock bottom prices.¬†

This was on the bucket list for a long time and finally ticked it off on a Saturday afternoon. As expected the place was full, although we were seated in a couple of minutes. Ambiance is minimal without air conditioning and sharing your table is a must like most of the small joints in North Kolkata.¬†

I tried the passion fruit, Cocoa Malai, Daab sarbat and Tamarind syrup based drink.¬†

The passion fruit is the costliest on the menu and it is clearly the winner. Its filling and tasted amazingly good. Prepared with rabri, almonds, cashew and raisins - this is a drink worth splurging (well as per Paramount standards ).¬†
The cocoa malai is chocolate based drink with a few almonds, cashew and raisins thrown in - tasted good too.¬†

The famous daab sarbat was refreshing and taste wise - the closest a drink can get to fresh coconut water.¬†

The tamarind syrup based drink was surprisingly good and a welcome change to the taste buds after the other items. I really really liked it and will definitely order this on my next visit.¬†

Pocket pinch for the 4 drinks - Rs 320. Sweet !¬†

Located in the lane behind College square, its best not to take a four wheeler as parking is an issue. Over all a great experience and totally recommended ! Cheers!

This place is a gem!!!Paramount was established in 1918 and at that time its name was 'Paradise'.This was a hidden meeting place for freedom-fighters.This is situated just at a perfect place where college students can go and relax.We ordered dab sharbat which was presented in a unique way.Dab Sharbat is a famous item of this place.Actually Acharya Sir Prafulla Chandra Ray proposed for Dab Sharbat so that students could have this as their tiffin at minimum cost.You can chitchat here and enjoy drinks.There are various sharbats and refreshments.This place is a historical place which you can feel sitting here.Of course prices are high.

2017-06-28 10:01:21
Ayesha
1519020
4.0
I visited the legendary "Paramount Sherbats and Syrups" with my mother yesterday after searching for books at the numerous book stalls . It was a hot summer afternoon and we figured that there was nothing better than a good glass of sherbat to cool off . It was a first for the both of us. I had read rave reviews about the place on Zomato and heard about it from some of my friends quite a few times. It was high time that I paid the place a visit during my next venture to college Street. The drinks cafe is located very close to the back gate of Calcutta University. It was packed with people trying to beat the heat when I walked in around 3 pm. The owner who sits at the desk at the front of the drinks cafe is very attentive to the needs of whoever comes in. The place is exactly like how I have imagined old cafes to be like. While maintaining its old world charm it continues to update its services by joining the swiggy network and putting up boards lit up to highlight the menu . The menu itself is comprehensive . Brief and to the point.

I had ordered a "cream pinapple" and my mother a "cream kesar lassi". Both of them were pretty good. The syrups used in each brought forward the respective flavours. Both were curd based and served with ice. Over the layer of ice was a white layer of a more buttery version of curd ( the layer that forms just below the soft crust of the malai.) It was to die for. I'd highly recommend the place to anyone who is in the area. It offers a break from the many cafes which serve shakes and smoothies. The sherbats here are something you won't find anywhere else in Calcutta because of the shere quality of ingredients used. Definitely visiting Paramount again to try more of their sherbats.

Update from 26.7.17
This time I had ordered a cocoa malai. It's a mix of milk, cadbury drinking chocolate , malai and dry fruits . I have never tried a blend of malai with chocolate milk before.....found it quite nice and refreshing . The service is pretty prompt as well. So if you're ever in college Street and have 10 minutes to spare , do drop into this place for a nice refreshing drink . Highly recommended.

2017-05-22 16:14:46
Ankita De
27721141
5.0
The beauty of Calcutta is so often tucked away in tiny streets, nooks and crannies.

Paramount is one such beauty, carefully preserved in an old gully behind College Square. 

I went to this little shop on a very hot afternoon with a friend. She insisted, thank God, she did. 

Once we secured a place, she promptly ordered three glasses of Dub Sarbat. 

When I looked at her, surprised, she just said, "wait, we'll divide one in half" and soon enough, I was thankful again.

The drink itself was cold, with a curious taste and very refreshing. Each glass had shreds of tender coconut kernels, to be scooped up and eaten with a spoon.

Paramount has kindled my curiosity about the other sarbats too. The essence of old Calcutta in a cool glass tumbler.

2017-05-21 09:49:51
Coolcandy Ankita
33062685
4.5
For my 100th review I chose this heritage sherbat joint that would be the best place to go to in this scorching heat! Following are the 5 items we tried from here:
1) dub(green coconut) sherbet(5/5)- well this is my first 5 points at anything...hands down the best sherbet that I have ever tried!! The plain green coconut water has a more intense taste here thanks to a syrup added(which btw is also sold individually). The liquid is further topped with green coconut kernel! A trip to this place from south Kolkata is justified by this drink alone!! MUST MUST TRY!!

2) kesar malai (3.5/5)- it's a kesar flavoured milkshake topped with kalakand ,malai(cream) and garnished with dry fruits! It's a great drink for kesar fans! It looks amazing too!

3) grape sherbat(2/5)- the most disappointing drink! It's an orangish brown coloured drink that had a sweet and sour flavour but I didn't find any familiarity with grapes...

4) green mango lassi(4/5)- this is a very refreshing version of a plain lassi! The creamy frothy lassi with a hint of green mango flavour! I Really liked it.

5)choco malai(4.5/5)- I am so glad we didn't leave before trying this one out! It is chocolate milkshake with a very strong flavour of cocoa and this too is topped with kalakand and dry fruits just that instead of using cream they used cocoa powder!! Highly recommended!!

The ambience is very different! One doesn't have a table for oneself but it's like there are benches on which people sit , side by side, for drinking their amazing sherbets together! I guess the very fact that There are people waiting to get a seat in a sherbet shop...speaks volumes about the popularity and quality of this place!

A unique place that must be visited by all!

Soumya Chakraborty thanks for introducing me to this place üòÉ and yet again thanks for being there beside me right from my 1st review!This one is dedicated to you!

2017-05-19 18:13:10
Dr. Bishal Kundu
32723962
4.5
Unique and one of its kind! Visited millions of times literally.
Best place for sherbats & chilled drinks. I've been here innumerable times.... Nearly every day during summer months, I visit this place. I have tried every item multiple times.
My personal favorite is Rose syrup...its taste , I don't know why , but its deep taste appeals to me with an excellent sensation all over the mouth. Rose malai & cream rose kind of dampens the flavour.
Cream green mango, dub sherbat, coca malai ...All are quite good.
Cream vanilla is also my favorite.
Tamarind syrup is amazing....The great refreshing taste is beautiful.
Khus khus syrup is also my one of the favorites. It's prepared from 'khus khus' (‡¶ñ‡¶∏ ‡¶ñ‡¶∏ ) , the thin slice of interwoven wood curtain that's hung on windows after soaking in water so that passing air gets cooled. A traditional air conditioner. When that 'khus khus' is still green ( just after made from mango tree), it's extract is taken to make the syrup. Its taste is really good & interesting...I can't actually describe in words.
Passion fruit also good....And very decorated. It's the extract of an exotic fruit named passion fruit, whose taste somewhat resembles that of Wood apple (‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶≤) , but is unique.
Grapes crush is also good & very calming.
Ambience feels good with memories of so many great personalities and awards.
It is one of the most unique food stops & a must visit place for tourists also.

Tucked away in the streets of north Kolkata is this legendary sherbat outlet. This store is one of the oldest and one of the best place that serves a variety of flavoured coolers that helps one to deal with the heat. For someone who visits college street this place is a must visit. There is a list of eminent people who have frequently visited this place and one feels privileged to share the space that was once shared by the celebrities.  Even today this place welcomes people from all ages, from all professions and its been able to live up to their expectations for ages.  
The seating arrangement is small and is mostly packed. Recommended drinks are 
1. DAAB SHERBAT - THIS IS MY FAVOURITE. Coconut water with daab malai, this drink gives all shakes a run for their money. And its very reasonable too.
2. Mango mania- mango flavoured shake with rabri, dry fruits that imparts a unique taste to this drink. 
3. Kesar Malai- drink is floured with saffron and rabri with loads of dry fruits 
4. Coco Malai- this chocolaty milkshake with rabri and dry fruits is really filling and refreshing...
If you are visiting college street, buy a couple of books, get a kobiraji from dilkhush or baked fish from coffee house or luchi cholar dal from putiram and then seal the deal with sherbat from paramount.  This completes your college street adventure :D

##

2017-05-01 09:54:14
Soumya Chakraborty
30477306
4.0
A legendary food establishment serving some of the best refreshments one can wish for. There is nothing ostentatious about this place, it is simple and commonplace yet there is a huge obsession amongst everyone to visit this place if they are in and around College Street area. The reason for this is the quality of the drinks they serve. It is located in one of the many lanes in College Street this place is always packed with customers. The students of the nearby schools and colleges form the majority of the crowd. I have been here many times over the years and there hardly seems to be any change in ambience or in the quality of service and servings. On my recent visit, I had ordered Dub Sarbat, Kesar Malai, Grapes Crush, Cream Green Mango, Cocoa Malai.

Dub Sarbat: Undoubtedly, the best drink I have ever had. Having this on a scorching summer day is pure bliss. This is a must try drink for all. Deftly prepared with coconut water and little bit of syrup with the kernel floating on top makes it an all-time favourite drink for all. Highly recommended!

Kesar Malai: This too is a very good drink. It is slightly heavy due to the presence of rubri, kheer and dry fruits. It is way better than the Frappes we get in CCD. This drink too is recommended!

Grapes Crush: This drink was slightly disappointing. It lacked the natural factor that this place is known for. It was too syrupy.

Cream Green Mango: Another great serving of this place. The cream provides a lassi kind of look and feel to this drink. The taste is exquisite. Recommended!

Cocoa Malai: A great drink with cadbury bits and dry fruits as toppings. This too is kind of heavy but you will enjoy it a lot. Recommended!

I have tried many of their other drinks and none disappointed me. This time, however, the grapes crush did not impress me at all. Others were all really good. The prices are extremely pocket friendly which makes it even better for the students. I would like to visit this place again and again.

##

2017-05-01 09:54:14
Soumya Chakraborty
30477306
4.0
A legendary food establishment serving some of the best refreshments one can wish for. There is nothing ostentatious about this place, it is simple and commonplace yet there is a huge obsession amongst everyone to visit this place if they are in and around College Street area. The reason for this is the quality of the drinks they serve. It is located in one of the many lanes in College Street this place is always packed with customers. The students of the nearby schools and colleges form the majority of the crowd. I have been here many times over the years and there hardly seems to be any change in ambience or in the quality of service and servings. On my recent visit, I had ordered Dub Sarbat, Kesar Malai, Grapes Crush, Cream Green Mango, Cocoa Malai.

Dub Sarbat: Undoubtedly, the best drink I have ever had. Having this on a scorching summer day is pure bliss. This is a must try drink for all. Deftly prepared with coconut water and little bit of syrup with the kernel floating on top makes it an all-time favourite drink for all. Highly recommended!

Kesar Malai: This too is a very good drink. It is slightly heavy due to the presence of rubri, kheer and dry fruits. It is way better than the Frappes we get in CCD. This drink too is recommended!

Grapes Crush: This drink was slightly disappointing. It lacked the natural factor that this place is known for. It was too syrupy.

Cream Green Mango: Another great serving of this place. The cream provides a lassi kind of look and feel to this drink. The taste is exquisite. Recommended!

Cocoa Malai: A great drink with cadbury bits and dry fruits as toppings. This too is kind of heavy but you will enjoy it a lot. Recommended!

I have tried many of their other drinks and none disappointed me. This time, however, the grapes crush did not impress me at all. Others were all really good. The prices are extremely pocket friendly which makes it even better for the students. I would like to visit this place again and again.

Whenever I visit College Street, I make sure to hop into Paramount for their daber sharbot. Almost a century old shop which only offers shorbots and range of syrups. ##

2017-03-04 22:53:01
Anisha Pal
35321131
4.5
94 years and still running strong! Paramount, located opposite college square is Kolkata's one of the oldest sherbet joints that serves you with instant happiness. That 4.5 is not just because of the boast worthy heritage, but also the lip smacking sherbets. Marble top tables, narrow benches, glass framed menus, walls adorned with wooden deer torsos and the photographs of famous people who had visited the shop, the ambiance is sheer nostalgia and creates the perfect atmosphere for an adda.¬†Coming to the sherbets, I was absolutely perplexed when asked to order because all of them looked equally tempting. I finally decided on the famous "Daab Sherbet" and the "Passion fruit sherbet". The daab sherbet was a refreshing one. It was topped with what we call 'daab er shaash' or ¬†coconut flesh. The passion fruit sherbet was rather an ornamental one. Generously topped with almonds, cashew and raisins, the sherbet had a thick layer of rabri. It was a filling and sumptuous drink. The price is very nominal and the people out there are always ready to welcome you with a smile and narrate the old stories related to the shop. You can also take home the syrups for a minimal cost. If one is in Kolkata, this is a must try shop.

##

2017-01-28 19:17:20
Shahrukh Ahmed
15540184
4.0
During the struggle for independence, the freedom fighters of our nation needed a hide-out and this is how this place is said to be formed. The Majumdars were said to sell coconut water (known by Daber Sherbat) in disguise just to keep the real motive hidden. After gaining independence, it turned itself into a full fledged 'sherbat' shop.

Going by the name, Paramount Sherbat and Syrups, it continues to thrive on and attract the attention of the masses. It is probably one of the rarest soft drink refreshment place where you find people flocking in off-season, too. The first visit to this place dates back more than half a decade ago when I just got shifted to Kolkata. A tution class acquaint asked me to accompany him while he was planning to pay this place a visit and out of courtesy I couldn't deny him. It turned out that this acquaint is now my dearest friend and well, it might be the effect of brotherhood that once thrived in the hearts of fighters but surely not the taste of the syrups.

This iconic shop is located on College Street just opposite to one of the gates of College Square and hardly few metres from the KMC office. It is spread over a tiny area with few wooden tables and chairs cluttered against each other and one always struggles to find place there being flocked by people of various ages almost all the time.

There are various types of sherbats and syrups available but all of them taste just fine with exception of drinks which are priced over ‚Çπ100. There isn't such a taste which will attracts folks from all corners but it's the history attached to it which makes it that popular. All the types of beverages that are provided here are just like any other shops serving the same and hence it doesn't justify the high price they charge.

However, I would like to mention that the grandchildren of Majumdar family who sits at the counter taking payments and listening to requests are very well behaved, polite and soft spoken. The courtesy one gets there are recommendable but the staffs doesn't always make you smile.

A visit is recommended!

So you can imagine how old and authentic the place is.

Place - Located at college street nearby coffee house... i guess i have nothing more to say about the heritage and popularity of the place.

2017-01-05 11:55:36
Bitan Banerjee
291684
4.5
This is not a regular place, this is a LEGEND. Successfully refreshing the minds and souls of people for more than 90 years, Paramount is a must visit for anyone in Kolkata. They have a wide variety of sherbets, each one competing with the others in the menu to win over the hearts of the people who come here. With a neat and archaic decor, one can have a feel that they are in a different Kolkata. My personal favourite is the Daab (Tender Coconut) Sherbet which you cant have one, you will definitely indulge into a second helping. They do serve sherbets without ice during most of the times in a year (not during Durga Puja though), so people with sore throats can also enjoy.

And in the restaurant business, customer satisfaction is highly sought, and Paramount is a pioneer in this. We wanted to have a second helping of the daab sherbet, but they ran out of coconuts. The lady who runs the place, took in the stride and made sure that we have another round of daab sherbet before we leave. I was appalled by this gesture, and my respect for this place increased 10 folds. You can also have sherbets take away, which they separately pack in a bottle for you. 

Paramount should be in the bucket list of all the citizenry of City of Joy and anyone who visits Kolkata.

2016-12-16 11:20:23
Diptajeet Datta
199112
4.0
Since 1918. Needs little introduction. I have been born and brought up in the vicinity of this place, so have seen and tried it since as long as I remember. This is no ordinary juice shop, it carries a lot of tradition. As I have tried this since my childhood, l like the taste of it. This is a family business and is into their 3rd generation now. I'm a little surprised that they haven't thought of expanding and restructuring the sitting place considering the huge amount of crowd it attracts. The service is fine and so is the ambience. The quality of the juices may has become a little different now but that can be accounted to multiple factors. Somehow the taste didn't stick this time. I always prefer the kesar malai and Daab sharbat. You can also opt for the Rose flavor based drinks, those are pleasant. Located just opposite to the college square swimming club complex, Paramount perhaps believes in retaining it's rich heritage and hence hasn't gone for a makeover. I like it the way it is and will keep going back as long as it's there.

4.0
A very urgent visit to the main campus of my university eventually drove me to the king of "sherbat cafes" in the city of joy through brisk serpentine steps. The sunrays were not that incandescent as the vintage-lover in me was ! For a few stable seconds, the camera of nostalgia rolled on and I almost stumbled upon two teenaged love-bird who were more than occupied between themselves to pay heed to anything else. Justified and unjustified. Especially when you are in the soft - drinks bar known as Paramount. Even people who are born and brought up in the Asansol-Durgapur belt won't confuse it with the most popular local confectionery......because this strip of shop in the very midst of Bankim Chatterjee street just alongside Mahabodhi Society is way too famous, even miles away. As the glimpses of my college-days blind faded away, I was dragged to reality and found myself alone for the first time in this shop. Cut the extra-literal part though.

Although I have planned and replanned to get truly enlightened with these strange delicacies newly introduced called "Passion of fruits" and "Litchi lassi", I geared up my extra-foodie genes to devour "Cocoa malai", my all-time favourite after "Dub-sarbat" and "Green mango lassi". As my eyes touched the left walls, the glamorous tabulation of their "ek-se-barkar ek" visitors from Day1 kicked my senses and hard-pinched the happy-go-lucky human being inside me.....and I remembered the jokes we shared that who amongst us would end up having his/her name enlisted over that antique chart. 

Did our beloved ex-captain of the cricket team ever dream of this honour? ?

I left with a rare pleasant smile with this thought in mind!

2016-09-23 18:47:25
Atindra Chakraborty
151379
2.5
This is a legendary place. It's located in the heart of College Street and is a must visit for all the people of Kolkata. They serve great sherbets,Lassis and syrups. I have tried almost 5 flavours by now and have never been disappointed once. 
However, this place is antiquated and seems like an anachronism in the year 2016.

It's very clumsy and dilapidated. The inside of it is very small and there is hardly any place to sit during rush hour. They don't accept cards and don't even intend to despite the enormous daily footfall.
Apart from the drinks there's nothing else to offer here. So, for everyone else still living in the past and suffering from the Golden age syndrome this place is an epitome of awesomeness. But as a realist I simply cannot be blind to the shortcomings of this place.

##

2016-08-13 09:49:18
Sayantani Sen
33029425
4.5
Cold drinks and syrups, best in town- next to none, proclaims the signboard outside. The claim is quite justified. Located on Bankim Chatterjee Street, just behind College Square, this is a historic place. My favourite is the Coco Malai, which is a cold chocolate drink loaded with dry fruits and with thick sweetened cream floating on top. This drink comes with both a straw to sip the drink, and a spoon to scoop out the solid goodies. When you think you have finished, if you fish among the ice chips at the bottom of the glass you are sure to find one or two pieces of nut. It is absolute heaven served in a glass. On a hot summer day, if you are both hungry and thirsty, coco malai is the perfect solution to all your troubles. It has always been the most expensive drink on the menu, the cheapest that I remember paying for it is Rs. 30, which has now increased to Rs. 100. However, the last time I went there I saw a new item on the menu called Passion Fruit which is even more expensive and the description says that it is made with rabri. I will definitely try that one day.
The less expensive drinks are also extremely popular- the daab sherbet particularly. The pineapple crush, green mango etc are curd based drinks. Though sometimes forced to drink these when I dont carry enough dough for the coco malai, I am not too fond of these myself because they all use a flavoured syrup which I find a little too sweet.
Paramount is a tiny little shop always buzzing with customers, but I have never seen the staff take more than 5 minutes to serve. It is quite an amazing place and if you do not visit it at least one in your life you have no idea what you are missing.

Paramount is very famous name for Lassi, Sarbat destination in Boi Para Area(College Street). Situated just behind of College Square Swimming pool and beside of Calcutta University Hall.

It is one of a legendary Lassi Destination, which doesn‚Äôt need any special intro and still operating from generation to generation for many years.

They served various kinda Sarbat, Lassi, Malai for many years. During my school life they had only few types of lassi, but the list is grown up with some good combination of lassi,.The main thing about their specialty is, the doesn't add any kinda preservative or color. So what you get is a total healthy and natural drinks.

Among all of them, Dab Sarbat is one my personal favorite sarbat out there. Served with Dab water, Dub Pulp and ice make this sarbat really healthy and refreshing also.

Green mango Lassi is also my very personal favorite lassi out there. Served with curd and green mango flavor and ice, which is really very tasty.

Coco Malai is the most expensive one among all sarbat. This is also a very unique one. You can try it.

¬†Ambiance is totally retro type, not so fancy. Basic table chair sitting. The place can hold a capacity of 25 Persons. Stuffs are very quick in serving your drink. Overall a very nostalgic experience.

2016-07-06 00:33:43

15738802
4.0
Don't go expecting anything less than deliciousness, 'cause you'll receive just that. This is one of those places, where you can feel years of history in the walls and the benches. Don't go in expecting decors and all that shiz, you won't get that! 

I've been there twice, and ordered the Cocoa Malai, Kesar Malai, Mango Mania,Dub Sarbat.

The Cocoa Malai is for chocolate lovers like me. It has a distinct Cadbury taste with generous amount of nuts and raisins. I'd have it time and again! It is quite filling and serves almost as a meal!

The Mango Mania is another super heavy shake with Rubri and nuts!! The mango flavour works very well with Rubri! Give this one a try with empty stomach and you'll enjoy this! 

Kesar Malai is the one with subtle flavour and classic Paramount feels.. 

Dab Sarbat.. Now this is the one with the utmost hype and you get why. On a hot sweaty day, after a haggle at College Street, this is the best thing that can happen to you! Coconut water, Soda, Basil and Mint in a perfect blend, what more can you ask for?!

This place has been, is and will be a part of Kolkata. Respect it!

##

2016-06-24 12:19:27
Indrajit Lahiri
542545
4.5
Somehow, I always felt, there lies multiple Calcutta inside our very own Kolkata. The city with its old world charm has always fascinated me along with the new-age facilities. In this hot scorching Indian summer, while finding a good cool drinks place, either we tend to end up at those numerous coffee shops with a glass of their unnecessarily pricey cold coffees/ smoothies or some lassi shops. But, where does Kolkata has to contribute here ? In this post, we‚Äôll be finding and discussing probably the oldest sherbet shop in Kolkata, who is still giving tough competition (with its very limited capacity and one of the strongest fan-base) to the above two- the Paramount.

Paramount lies at the corner of Collage square on Bankim Chatterjee St, just after the Mahabodhi Society. Its generally open throughout the year (because of strong customer demand) from Monday- Saturday 11 AM-9 PM. The good part of these bengali food joints is, as soon as you enter, you magically get transported to some magical era of old-world charm, an era where people used to be polite and a certain ‚ÄúBhodrota‚Äù/ subtlety used to surround them. Such is this place. The place is a small room with stone-top tables and chairs. In the billing counter, you can find a small, fragile lady taking care of the billing needs. This place seems to be one of those very few place in Kolkata, where the entire operation is taken care by the Majumder family members and not depending on the external resources-thus keeping a strong check on the quality.

Once you settle down on those rickety wooden benches, you‚Äôll be asked for your choice and mind it, the server gentleman will expect you to know your choice without even looking at the elaborate menu Now, that‚Äôs the way it works here and after running the establishment for almost 100 years, it can‚Äôt be changed. At this point of time, trust me and go for their Dub sherbet. at least to buy you the time to think for the next items. Its pure orgasm. Dub water and vanilla flavored sherbet with tender coconut extracts floating, you‚Äôll need a spoon (which actually they provide) with the straw. Leave the straw and sip secretly wishing, you could‚Äôve mixed with a little vodka. Worry not traveller, you can buy this thing home in their nice packaging and can have it with a dash of Smirnoff.

Once you‚Äôre through with their thin sherbets, yo may like to move on to their cream based malai segment and in this scorching summer, what better than mango malai ? Again, you‚Äôll be tempted for Cocoa malai and Vanilla malai, so I would suggest to go in a group (at least with few of GF/ BF‚Äôs- to split the offerings). All are good, but I have a special soft spot for Mango Malai. But frankly, I didn‚Äôt like the dry fruits of top (more kinda non-bong touch), otherwise brilliant.

But, after all this sweetness, you might link something less sweet and the management has though of that also, the have tamarind sherbet and green mango. The tamarind and green mango extract is produced in-house and hence free from all harmful ingredients. The Tamarind sherbet is more tangy and spicy lovemaking (its a make or break situation) wherein Green Mango is more like a subtle first kiss with curd base with the extract.

¬†Tamarind sharbat Green mango sharbat

By this time, you should be quite full (both appetite-wise and pocket-pinch-wise). Let me warn, none of these items are cheap, by any means but the cost is justified. Where else, you can get a shop dedicated to sherbet, with proper seating arrangement, a waiter and a proper billing system ? People has been enjoying their favorites here from decades and Majumder family has been servicing them since them, knowing their individual preferences. So, let‚Äôs join in and enjoy

Located towards the end of college square, this tiny sit down eatery that serves only cold beverages has been around for over a century now. The place is a legend when it comes to sherbats and syrups.

Crushed grapes was the another favourite that we devoured before we decided that finally our hearts were full.

2016-05-31 05:02:48
The Foodinista
31649667
5.0
Whenever I visit College Street I make it a point to visit Paramount - the one-stop shop for sherbets in Kolkata . Paramount is a 98 years old sherbet joint that boasts of a rich heritage that very few places in the city can match up to. It is declared as a Heritage building/shop by Kolkata Municipal Corporation. 

The most popular and the best sherbet in Paramount is the¬†Daber Shorbot¬†- a¬†Sharbetmade of tender coconut water, ice, syrup and the white meat/pulp of the coconut. Once you take a sip of Daber¬†Sharbat¬†you will understand why people prefer Paramount's¬†Sherbet¬†than any regular soft drinks to quench their thirst.

The menu includes Green Mango, Cream Vanilla, Cocoa¬†Malai, Rose¬†Malai, Passion Fruit, Grape Crush, Strawberry¬†Malai, Tamarind and Lichi other than the famous and refreshingly delicious¬†Daaber Sharbat. I generally start with Daaber Sarbat¬†and then have other¬†Sharbets and then end with Green Mango.


So all in all Paramount is a treat to your taste buds and is a true symbol of Kolkata‚Äôs past glory and heritage. The LIVING LEGEND !

Paramount is a stone throw away from my home. I have been visiting this place since my childhood. And I take great offense if someone says it is hyped or what not! The line on the hot summer days always prove the haters wrong. But as the saying goes haters gonna hate and the potatoes gonna potatet. :-P
PJs apart you have to come here once. I am not a curd fan so I will not be commenting on the curd based drinks. I am a die hard fan of the cocomalai. Now Rs 100 a glass. It is a pocket pinch. U started having this when it was rs 25 a glass so I completely feel it when my father says things during his time were so cheap. But then again to enjoy good things in life one has to shell out.

CocoaMalai:- must try for everyone. A chocolate based drink topped with a thick layer of malai and cashews and raisins. Scoop the malai with the spoon and slurp on the drink. When the small cashew pieces block your straw, blow on it once. :-P it works. 

Cold coffee:- another classic. It tastes like normal cold coffee but not thinned down with water. 

They had introduced a tamarind drink. Mind blowing. If you like phuchka water then you would love this one. Chilled tamarind drink. Perfect for this weather. 
 This is a must visit for all the foodies.

##

2016-03-31 16:49:36
Dipyaman Basu (whenstomachtickles)
627356
5.0
Some people do not need praises likewise some food establishments do not require compliments to establish their supremacy. Not that they are ¬†over-zealous about their achievements but people know the fact that they have always been that good to reign the hearts of millions of people residing in Kolkata since many years now.

In this current ultra-modernized society, when sitting on an 'Adda' implies walking into cafe's to puff over a Shisha or sipping your throats over a fancy-named Mocktails, there also exists a conservative section of people who still prefer to do things, the 'Old-Way'! Which means sitting on the roadside with a paperbag of Telebhaja in hands or sitting inside a not-so-fancy looking outlet to spend some precious time over a glass of cold 'Shorbot'!

Tucked inside one of the lanes around College Square/College Street, this is one of few shops which defined the very essence of Bangaliana. A trip to this area is not completed, unless you feed yourselves with the enticing Telebhajas at Kalika and then finish your meal with a satisfying glass of Serbats at Paramount. The history of this outlet goes way back. For some, this shop exists even before we were born.

Although the menu isn't much elaborate here, it pretty much has all the varieties one would want! Start with their refreshing Coconut (Dub) Sarbat, which is undoubtedly the biggest hit in this place. Cool sip of coconut water with chunks of 'Malai. Although, try not finish off the Malai as soon as you start. Instead keep having it as you sip your way to the bottom of the glass.

You want something exotic? Go for Passion Fruits, Coco Mania or Mango Malai. You want some curd based drinks? Go for Cream Green Mango or Cream Lassi. These people have it all. As you sit there taking all your time to enjoy the refreshments and enjoy in a conversation with your buddies, you would see names and pictures of several iconic and legendary figures who have visited here in the past and probably has enjoyed the same drinks you are feasting upon now with the same vibe and enthusiasm.

The staffs are super-friendly here and so is the owner. The charge here is pretty nominal and they also provide fresh plastic bottles at a marginal rate if you plan on packing some of their delicacies back home. The interior is nice and clean with no hygiene issues. The only con here is their heritage and popularity tag, due to which, the place gets super-flooded at times, and hence securing a seat may be the next difficult thing in the world other than to impress the girl you love!

##

2016-03-05 22:43:21
Sreejata Chakraborty
2562482
5.0
This small, nondescript, little hole of an outlet off College Street is one of those innumerable things which makes Calcutta such an amazing city. Serving some of the best Sherbets in town, Paramount is one of the must-visit places in the city for residents and tourists alike. While one doesn‚Äôt really need to know the specials for a place like this, since no matter which drink you choose, it‚Äôs going to be a soul-pleasing, heart-soothing savior for your parched throat on a stuffy Calcutta afternoon- the Daab Sherbet deserves special mention which is a wonderful concoction of the fresh, tender, sweet Malai (Leyi- in Bengali) of a coconut and its sweet water and some of their other special syrups. The Daab Sherbet is so good that it gets sold out very fast and one has to wait a considerable amount of time before they replenish their stock and are ready to serve again. The service is fast, attentive, the seating area small and the atmosphere casual. It is one of those no-nonsense places which serves amazing stuff at throwaway prices and has a cult following not only in Calcutta but almost in the entire Bengali Diaspora. The walls of Paramount are lined with Newspaper cuttings of prominent Authors like Jhumpa Lahiri, Arundhati Roy etc. enjoying their Saab sherbet at Paramount. 

So, Paramount is not just a normal run-of-the-mill little place which serves drinks but an institution which has been a silent witness to all the rebellions rising out of neighboring Presidency College and Calcutta University.

##

2016-02-01 20:39:35
Sumit Surai
11641
4.0
Whenever I am around College Street area, I try not to miss this place. Paramount has a lot of history attached to it. But what's more important is, they have managed to keep people hooked with their refreshing drinks.

Daab Sharbat is their most famous item, and according to me a must try. It is tender coconut drink with pieces of tender coconut flesh floating on it. Absolutely divine and thirst quenching.

The Ghols or the cream (curd based) drinks are next best items for me. Cream green mango and cream lemon are my personal favourits, though I love Cream orange too.

I am not a big lover of only syrup and water drinks, but love the tamarind drink from this section. Refreshing!

Passion fruit I order rarely as it is very heavy. Make sure you have an empty stomach before you order this. With Rabri and dried fruits, this is on the sweeter side too.

Most of the days I start with a Daab Sharbat and then order any two of the cream based drinks and end with another Daab, occasionally adding a tamarind in between.

Paramount Sherbats & Syrups - Paramount in literal sense means supreme or say something which is of great importance. This place has been rightly named.¬†
=====
Intro + Location: It might be a little difficult to locate this place but i will make it easy for you guys. ¬†Enter Lane Opposite to Presidency Uni/College and take the first Right. On the left food after walking for say 2 minutes, you will discover this. This place does not have a board but the name is so famous that if you ask anyone, people will guide you through. It is one of the oldest sherbat shop and i think it is established in 1918 if i am not wrong. Most of the prominent personalities like Amartya Sen, Netaji Subhash Chandra Bose etc etc. and even our famous cricketer Sourav Ganguly has paid a visit. When anyone speaks about paramount, it is about their famous daab sherbat.¬†

I did expect a signboard for Paramount at the top which was not there. However, they were busy constructing the other part of the building to enlarge their scale of operations. I took my seat and somehow this place did give me a really peaceful feeling. The ceilings and fan reminded me of my old home in Bhawanipur. Nevertheless, it could have been cleaned a bit on the walls and ceilings to remove the spider webs. They have also put a lot of wall photos of Rabindranath Tagore, Swami Vivekananda and many more prominent people.¬†
=====
What i ordered:¬†

‚Ä¢ Grapes Crush - It was good. However, the syrup was added a lot more than it should be making it a bit more sweet than usual. ¬†‚úå

‚Ä¢ Daab Sherbat - This sherbat definitely is something really worth tasting. I had been hearing from many of my connoisseur friends and somehow, i did get to try it finally. It's usual daab water mixed with their syrup and ice to top. Tasted extremely good and i went on ordering another one. I also packed the Sherbat in the Bottle they gave me. It was really worth it. ‚úå
=====
Pros:

‚Ä¢ This place feels like home.¬†
‚Ä¢ The owner is friendly.¬†
‚Ä¢ The service is fast as they only cater to sherbats and juices etc etc.
‚Ä¢ It is a very old establishment. More like a brand name now.¬†
‚Ä¢ Seating area is just fine. They are expanding too.¬†

Cons:

‚Ä¢ The place could have been kept more clean specially the ceilings and walls.¬†
=====
Expert Suggestion:
‚Ä¢ Please put a board on the outside so that people can highlight your outlet. This will help you gain additional customers.
=====
Sherbat for two 150-300 max
=====
Conclusion: I would love to pay a visit again. This place feels like home. Really a good place to have some sherbat and chill. ¬†‚ù§
=====
Unbiased review based on my visiting experience. 
=====
Recently, went there and had tamarind and daab sherbet. Tamarind is also a good try if you want tangy flavour.

Ladies and gentlemen.. Boys & Girls ..

1. Dub Sharbat ( 5/5 )
2. Kesar malai ( 4/5 )

Well if you are asking whats kesar malai sherbet is all about . It is a combo of ( Rubri + Milk + Kheer + cashew nuts + ice = awesomeness ) . Its like the malai portion of rasomalai inside a full glass with ice . Trust me it is glorious. Priced at at a slight hefty 100 rupees this juicy delight is one for the memories. But the real show stopper is the Dub Sherbet . I would not describe it much in words because you just have to experience it yourself . If you are in Bengal or an outsider you have to test this once in a lifetime . The dub sherbet is as legendary as it gets. I will certainly go there again and again and again .. and each time i will have one choice as constant - The Dub Sherbet . :)

2015-11-09 21:19:55

5.0
Paramount doesn't need an introduction amongst the old generation that grew up with College Street books. Every time I visit College Street, it's a must for me, summer or winter. But the summers make it just amazingly delightful. 

It's a small shop with a fair bit of old school ambience to it. Coming to the sherbets, the Cocoa Malai is the king of the ring and the undisputed champ. The super tasty drink with a very generous doze of nuts is just amazing.

But there is something about the Orange sherbet that I love. It's got a rather strong flavour of sour that gives an amazing kick followed by a lovely dash of sweet. I always end up having a couple of them or more. 

I only wished they had more branches to fulfil my insatiable thirst for amazing sherbets. Nevertheless, it's always worth the trip to the other side of town for this beauty.

I won't waste my words trying to describe how the tantalizing the sherbat is... Instead I would just stick to the words,,, "Paramount : the age old name in sherbats ."¬†
Being from Kolkata certain places are ingrained in your growing up years in food wise or drink wise .. This place certainly ranks high in the list.. It is the most iconic place of North Kolkata who thrived on food joint like Coffee house, located in the heart of the College Street.."College Street" the word is enough to describe that the legendary place z how much popular among the college goers & the book lovers..¬†
Regardlessly to say, this place more than lives upto its name.. This place gives you the feel of true Bangaliana, the decor akin an old zamindar bari jzt adds to the old world charm with high ceilings, deer head bust wall hanging that date as far back as 1918.. Its walls are adorned with the different articles.. Though its not have an extraordinary ambiance like nowadays cafeterias along with exotic names of drinks on the menu..¬†
I went to this place with my friend to quench my thirst. I have almost tried everything from their menu chart but cocoa malai and Daab (coconut) sherbat is actual coconut water with the daab malai on top, are my personal favorite..¬†
Paramount is just like heaven in a hot summer afternoon & the crowd moves so fast u really don't have to wait for long.. And about their price chart if you compare it with the other parlour or juice stop, then you won't notice much of a difference..The place.. The staff... The quality.. The taste.. Has all remained the same... Its like a frame fixed in time..

5.0
Had been to the place on 18th of september with a friend of mine. The place is located close to umesh chandra college on college street. The place has sitting arrangments and looks very old. 

The people at the place are very hospitable and the lady at the counter welcomes you with a big smile. We ordered for a cocoa malai , dab sharbat, cream rose and kesar malai. The dab sharbat was the best. The sharbat has pieces of coconut cut and put in the sharbat and it really tastes amazing. You should defenitely try this one if you ever visit the place. The cocoa malai is also faboulous. Cream rose is made with curd base so it is salty and not sweet but yes it tastes great. Although i personally didnt like the kesar malai much as compared to the others.

The price is slightly on the higher side although they do not charge any tax over the prices displayed in the menu, but the shebats there are worth every penny spent. A must go place for all people who love drinking sherbats.

Paramount is THE perfect place to cool down after a stint at book hunting.
The store is a bit small, traditional type with simple benches. The ambience is simple, and nothing much to talk about. Thing to note is the big board with list of famous people who have visited Paramount over the ages.

But hey, you don't come here for the ambience, you come here for the Sherbets.
The Daab Sherbet and the Green Mango Syrup are my favorite, and must tries. They are cool and pleasing, will freshen you up instantly.
Prices are pretty reasonable, might seem steep on paper, but you really need to experience it to understand the value.

Oh, did I mention, that after 2 years, Paramount will be 100 years old!!!!

Paramount isn't just another shop, its a legacy, a trip down memory lane, an experience in itself.

Update 28 Oct'15

Went back to the place after many years with a friend. The place is still the same as it's used to be in my school years. Standing on the sands of time the shop seems younger by the years. 

I ordered for a mango mania and my friend a cold coffee. Taste was as per the standards of paramount. I felt ice was used more than required.

Old post:
In the heart of college street lies one of most famous Sherbat ka Dukan ( juice shop). I grew up in the area and for many childhood years it was way out of our league. Then in layers years we friends often opted for a one or two drinks here. I tasted various conventional drinks like mango, orange, rose and some special ones. E.g. Dab er sorbot, badam lassi, and off course the famous original lassi with a layer of papercurd over the top. If you're around the area do check out this place. It is a bit difficult to locate from a nonregular customer. Ask around and many will come for you help. The shop is right behind Hindu School near to the back exit of College Square.

2015-07-27 08:36:51
Monami Basu
30342916
4.5
I first went here with my best friend Kakali when we were studying MA in University of Calcutta. It was a long time ago. We were impressed by the marble topped tables and stuffed animal heads and old photos. It was a sultry afternoon and we were thirsty. Kakali chose rose sherbet. I wanted to try Cocoa Malai, but at that time it was Rs18/-, too expensive to try, so I chose Dab sherbet instead. Kakali later regretted that rose sherbet was nothing but rose syrup with ice, she had the idea that rose sherbet would contain real rose petals! I did not regret my choice. It was a wonderful refresher with a piece of dab malai floating inside the glass.
Days passed on. I often went there during my student days, with or without friends. Tried the other sherbets, including rose sherbet, and loved each one of them. However, cocoa malai, the costliest sherbet, remained a distant reality.
Even after my student days were over, whenever I went to College Street, I would come here for a drink, and one day I tried Cocoa Malai. By that time the price had risen, but I could afford it. It was like heaven, much better than ordinary ice cream or any other dairy products that I had tasted earlier. I promised myself to visit the place again and again.
In 2012, I went there last with my parents. We all chose cocoa malai. However I was disappointed at the fact that they did not serve it in the tall glass they used to serve. The glass was short, and the taste was not what it used to be. The quality has been reduced drastically. The price has also gone up. I wanted my ailing father to enjoy but he thought that we could have made better choices.
However, the ambience, the marble topped tables etc still remain, giving a feeling of nostalgia, reminding me of those light hearted student days.

2015-07-20 00:05:10

4.5
The tradition of coconut water in north and central Kolkata has been eminent since ages and this is being upheld fondly by Paramount too. Sourcing the coconuts from Basirhat, one gets to experience a refreshing coolness with the Daab Sherbet that's a blend of fresh tender coconut water, sugar syrup, essence and loads of crushed ice. It's light, tasty, definitely a thirst quencher that leaves you wanting for more!
Coco Malai is definitely one of Paramount's popular draws that's loaded on the Malai front. It's laced with dry fruits to complement the cocoa flavour with sweet malai base. I definitely like to finish off any of the drinks with the Daab Sherbet again!!
The decor/seating might not be posh like an upscale CCD or Barista the old era marble top tables with lined walls of eminent guests adorn the rich heritage of Paramount. Interestingly they do have a placard stating, "If you like it, tell others. If you don't like, tell us" ! We did just that; we found our Coco Malai to be on the bland side and asked to be improvised and voil√†! They whipped in some more Malai and magic and we were two happy, eternal Paramount fans, yet again!!

##

2015-07-14 13:14:14
Sreyasree Dutta
3050422
4.5
A long, long walk from CR Avenue to College Street for books, and more walking thereafter, we entered Paramount with exhausted legs and thirsty souls. On sitting we were handed the cards and I was immediately confused about what to leave out. 
Fortunately, the lady at the counter, who was just wonderful, helped us out. I finally settled with a cream orange and my companion, a cream green mango. 
It wasn't two minutes before our drinks were served. 
Creamy, cold, tangy, fruity, not too sweet, they were perfect. The green mango did taste a lot like the pineapple yogurt from mother dairy (just to give a reference to the lovely flavour). My cream orange was actually orangey but not at all artificial, and not too tart.
Then we went bonkers. And ordered the mango mania. And it was so, very worth the splurge. Loaded with rabri, malai and a generous dose of dry fruit with full fat milk with a generous amount of mango pulp, it was a revelation. Mango milk never tasted this good! We fought for the last drop, and were left wishing that had it were more.
I ended up taking a pineapple malai for mom, and even though she had it lukewarm four hours later, it still was creamy and perfectly sweet. She liked it so much that she refused to part with it at all! 
Our total bill came to 210 bucks, and even at first sight the drink price may look steep, but the goodness there is undeniable. And they really fill you up, unlike most beverages, more so if you request them to make it without ice. 
Bliss in a glass, thy name is Paramount!

2015-07-02 16:36:44
Keka De
258874
5.0
This place never disappoints - all the times that we've been there - be it that first time, when i walked in with wide-eyed wonder holding Baba's hand or trooped in later with my friends from college - Paramount has always quenched our soul's thirst.
I always start with a glass (or two) of the awesome Daab Sharbat and then move on to the Green Mango or Vanilla or Rose Sharbats... I have never tried the Coco-Malai (nor do I want to) but I always think of trying the Grape Sharbat but veer away at the last moment... some day, eh?
The ambience is old-world and welcoming - the decor consists of sturdy wooden benches and marble topped tables which are always cool and welcoming, and the omnipresent antlers mounted on the wall. There are framed newspaper articles all over the place, from yellowing pieces which talk about how a Subhash Bose loved their fare to a new one of some PYT posing with a glass of sharbat. The lineage of their Syrups is impeccable - the Daab Sharbat syrup was supposedly formulated by the venerable Acharya Prafulla Chandra Roy. Now, who can fault credentials like that?They have also started a takeaway service where you can carry away 2 or 3 glasses worth of sharbats in cute plastic bottles for an extra charge.
The Daab Sharbat is definitely the star of the show - with pieces of tender coconut floating in the special syrup mixed with coconut water and ice shavings. Try it once, and you'll be coming back for more!

##

2015-06-23 22:38:01
Debajyoti (www.foodiedada.com)
1855976
4.5
Very few people have actually heard of Nihar Ranjan Majumdar‚Äôs 'Paradise sherbet shop'. But when I start talking about Paramount Sherbets everyone will surely be able to recognize this legend. Name has changed but the place still remains the same, and definitely the quality remains as it is. This legendary sherbet and juice bar still retains the old world charm and teleports you several decades back when you step right in. 

Location ---- Located at Kolkata's 'boi para', this place is next to the Mahabodhi Society (opposite College Square) and the place is infact quite close to the Putiram sweet shop.

Beverages ---- On my last visit (infact I was at Collge street with one of my foodie friends just to spend some time at Paramount!) I tried my favourite below two drinks:

a) Dub Sarbat: It is a refreshing concoction made of sweet soothing coconut-water, the pulp of the tender coconut, crushed ice and some secret syrup. It is a pure joy to try out this drink and I generally take less than one minute to finish off the first glass of Dub Sarbat on a hot summer day! As a matter of fact, this drink was famous even in 1918 when the shop just started operating. Back then the summer coolers (specially the Dub Sarbats) were served to the public and in the backgound something big was actually going on since this place was a hideout for freedom fighters and I have heard that there was one secret room for them at this place! Infact it is said that recipe for this dub sherbet was actually then prepared by the famous scientist Acharya Prafulla Chandra Ray!  

b) Green Mango: This is the best refreshing drink I have ever tried. It is made from mango extract, some essence, sugar, salt and crushed ice. If you are here at Paramount then surely do try one glass of Green Mango, it'll be a crime if you don't; infact that is true for the Dub Sarbat as well :)

Ambiance ---- The humble settings, old furnitures, high ceiling fans and old wall hangings give that warm feeling and makes you feel blessed and nostalgic at the same time. It is a small shop and the place is naturally quite cramped up, but when you are here you are actually in a time warp and the thrill is enough to ignore all these petty issues.  

Hygiene ---- Though you may feel that it is not safe to have road-side sarbats, etc on hot summer days, but this is Paramount and things are quite different here. They don‚Äôt use synthetic materials in their beverages and the ingredients are primarily derived from fruit extracts, infact the ice used is being sourced from the same supplier all thoughout these 97 years! The table tops where the drinks are served are made of white marble and are generally kept clean.

Price and Service ---- Nothing much to say, the price at this place has always been very reasonable and it's truly worth every penny. There are no additional taxes charged. The service is very prompt and orders are readily taken and served almost in proper sequence.

Overall ---- The common meeting place for revolutionaries involved in the Swadeshi Movement like Netaji Subhas Chandra Bose, Pulin Bihari Das, Satin Sen, etc is still standing tall today with all its rich heritage serving those signature beverages and summer coolers to all the die-hard fans, some of them are again legends like Satyajit Ray, Uttam Kumar, Suchitra Sen, Bikash Ray, Shibram Chakraborty, Balaichand Mukhopadhyay, S.D. Burman, and so on. As of today the place highly depends on word-of-mouth advertising and is still going strong even after nearly 100 years! We hope and pray that this Beverage Museum goes strong for the coming 100 years... and more. Long live the legend!

Cheers!

2015-06-06 16:13:12
Arindam Bhattacharjee
1046543
5.0
Some things are life are so replete with their existence yet so rare in their true essence. Paramount is such a place. You want to know North Kolkata, the true Kolkata? Start by sipping down a drink at Paramount. You watch the hand-pulled rickshaw ply by, book hawkers wavering their hands from their tiny stalls, you watch the occasional nerd with his books, the hormonal teen with his girlfriend and the thousands of literary titles grabbing your attention everywhere just when a tram tries to ram you mid-road. 

It's sensory overload. 

And then you either go cool down splashing water at the College sq. pool; or you take a sip of the elixir that they serve you here. And they know you enjoy a cold drink best when you're hot so they don't have ACs. And then the stuffed antler head, the narrow benches, the handwritten signs.. It's not vintage 2.0. It's vintage 1.0. And nobody does it better than Paramount. 

P.S. Doesn't matter what you order, but my favorite is the coco malai.

##

2015-04-12 23:17:51
Sufi
295715
4.5
Well...a very tiny place but loadz of reason to admire. I hit up this place with one of my friend on a bright summer sunday morning... We had been walkin for 30 minz under scorching sun and the day was quite humid too. So, no other day could be much more approprite to drop by at Paramount... But... Reaching there ...realized... quenching thirst won't be that easy ... After all...good things are not easily earned :p ... After knocking there, we were informed that the juice parlour is closed and would get opened around 4 o'clock in the evening... We talked to the Owner and told that we have come all the way to have sharbat @paramount ... noticing the keenness in us to have a sip in the sharbats, the courteous propreitor allowed us in and suggested us to try their's signature glass ... Daaber sharbat (Tender coconut Juice)... Since the shop was not open so it took time for the glasses of chilled sharbats to arrive...though we didn't get bored...as we had an interesting talk with the owner Mr. M. Mojumder ...trust me guyz... I have never come across such a courteous , humble and nice proprietor whoes eatry is so eminent. Now...coming to the sharbat... I can bet that this daaber sharbat can't be found in any other place of India.. . It tastes  heavenly and gives an instant bliss the moment you have the first sip and it continues till the very last drop... I would love to land up here again and again.
N.B. (for all those gourmets who are inquisitive about the legends behind dishes and eatry) : The discussion with the Owner , was quite insightful... He is the 2nd generation running this business. His father had started this with the name Paradise sharbat which used to be a secret meeting place of freedom fighters . In the year 1937 it got banned by British government and later was reopend in the name of Paramount... Also, another interesting fact is that the "Daaber sharbat" was a recipe from Acharya Prafulla Chandra Roy... So the Paramount is not only a treat to your taste buds or thirsty throat but also a true insignia of Kolkata‚Äôs past glory and heritage.

##

2015-04-07 12:16:14
Saurodeep Basak
1507076
4.0
This restaurant has been around since since 1918.Till today it is run by the same family who started it. The third generation is running it now. Incredible ‚Äì that‚Äôs what keeps it going. The shop has a list of famous people of Bengal who have visited this shop. Some of the names include netaji subhash Chandra Bose, Satyajit Ray, Meghnad Saha, Jagadish Chandra Bose, Uttam Kumar, Suchitra Sen, etc. The ceiling of this old building is obviously ‚Äòkori kaath‚Äô ‚Äì metal & wood beams that was characteristic of buildings of that time. The concept of this restaurant is interesting. A sharbat store with proper seating arrangement like a restaurant, servers coming & taking order & serving the sharbat - quite unique I must say! I have visited here a million times (each time with different company). So today I am reviewing my latest visit.¬†

The co-owner lady like every time suggested some good sherbets. We started with Daab sharbat. Marvellous. Daab water formed the base. The malai of coconut was floating in the sharbat. We were given spoons to enoy the malai. The sharbat was thickened a bit from the daab water texture & was flavoured as well. The external vanilla like flavor & the daab flavor both made their presence felt.¬†

We moved on to Green mango sharbat. The concentration of this has been made by them in-house. The Green mango sharbat tasted a bit like the synthetic green mango jelly that is available in the market. This sharbat was in a dahi base. Tasted very good on its own but very different from what I thought it would be.¬†

Next sharbat we had was Tamarind sharbat. This turned out to be the best in the lot. Intense taste & flavor. Great balance of sweet, salt & sour. Very good flavor of tamarind. It was simply marvelous.¬†

Lichu sharbat was recommended by the lady. It was wonderful as well. A tad more sweet but outstanding flavor of lichi. Sucked it till the last drop!¬†

Last sharbat we had was milk based ‚Äì Kesar malai. This one turned out to be sub optimal when compared to thick & rich North Indian Doodh based sharbats. The one at Paramount was average in taste and quite "diluted" in consistency. Though it had some malai onto it, but it didn't the drink. The only letdown so far.¬†

Quite naturally, this isn't my final visit. I will be visiting here countless times with new people and new memories!

Now comes the menu - 10/10 for the Dub Sarbat. This is a chillar - a fresh jump-start to your battery when you are tired and out of energy. They have just blended the perfect drink.

Cocoa malai is tremendously rich will lots of cashew, almond, pista and a creamy rich smooth drink. One of the best recommended. I have had almost all the malai varieties that are served over here and also most of the cream ones. By best is pineapple malai and cream green mango.

Do the place need renovation? I would suggest No, it is good as it is. The old decor - a symbol of the bygone days of Kolkata when it was Calcutta - and the nostalgia of eating at a place which was once infested by the likes of Subhash Bose, Satyajit Ray, JC Bose, Uttam Kumar etc.

Overall hugely recommended and a perfect 5/5 for this place.

Was planning on visiting this place for a long time. Finally went there today with a friend. It's located just behind college square.
The ambiance is typically that of north Calcutta. The warmth with which they serve their customers is truly amazing. The thing that I especially liked about this place is inspite of being such an old joint its spotlessly clean and not shabby unlike coffee house. Maintainance is superb.
Now coming to the juice we had ordered one cocoa malai and one dub shartbat as I have heard numerous stories about these two. The choco malai was too good. The chocolaty sharbat with malai on the top sprinkled with cocoa powder and cashews is worth dying for. Dub shartbat had bits of coconut skin in it and tasted awsum. Pure bliss.
Service is very prompt and they ask for feedback and suggestions which is probably why they have sustained all over these years. The owner is very cordial and on learning that we were 1sr timers there he took special care of us.
They even have a list of the names of eminent personalities who have visited this place. It consists of names of ppl like Acharya prafulla Chandra roy and the famous dub sherbat was actually his favorite.
Overall a great experience. U'll get CCD and Baristas everywhere u go but this is truly a gem of a place with its old world charm which serves traditional and authentic sharbats at damn cheap price. Will b revisiting to try out the other varieties. Great expectations from here. Keep up the good work:-)

2014-12-10 15:04:19
Shakri Banerjee
46054
3.5
You enter Paramount and instantly you are transported back to a bygone era, a yesteryear's Kolkata. Some places are heritage, this place is one such place. You take the lane opposite to Presidency University main gate, travel the length of College Square, take a right and the place falls on your left side after about 10 feet walk. The tables are age old, with white marble tops that are always clean, instead of chairs you find small wooden benches to sit. The walls are adored with old photographs. ¬†Even the Sign outside is as old as the shop. My all time favorite choice is the Cocoa Malai. A frothy milky drink that is topped with crushed khowa kheer and sprinkled with chocolate (cocoa) powder. ¬†Recently, I am seeing that they have added some new mixes on the menu like Vanilla Malai and Banana Malai (!!!). Earlier it just used to be Cocoa Malai and Rose Malai. The Passion Fruits is also a new addition and looks inviting. Have to visit to try that. The Daab Sarbat is the signature. Its very soothing on a hot summers day when you are parched to your core. But I sometimes find it too sweet.¬†
Some places are great due to their sheer presence, due to their resistance to change, due to their fondness of the old. Although I see the management has revamped the menu quite a bit, I just hope that they have not replaced the heritage character of this place.

With the time Paramount is coming out with new innovative tasty flavours of Sherbats, but the Dub Sherbat is the only one of its kind, you will never find this one any where else, each and every time I visit Paramount I never ever missed a single time to order this one except this onet he Green Mango, Coco Malai, Passion Fruit Malai, is a must try. You have to visit quite a few times to try all the flavours.¬†
Personally recommend all food lovers to give this one at least one try, I am sure you will visit the place once again.

I can't believe that the people of Kolkata gave so cold-hearted review about this place. No, I did not study in any institution around College street, but I have¬† very emotional bond with this shop. 

Tip #1: Go there thinking it as a museum.

Tip#2: Talk to the owner(s).

Tip#3: Appreciate the 100-years-old imported Italian marble table tops and the Deer horns. Notice that one of those tables does not have the same table top. Ask the owner why not. Ask who discovered the Daab Sherbet.

Do you know what Sherbet means? It means to welcome. Paramount taught me that. There are things beyond business. North Kolkata reminds you of that, and to truely appreciate the sherbet of Paramount, you would have to learn that. E Kolkatar majhe achhe ar ekta Kolkata.

4.0
The moment you step into Paramount you feel transported to an era bygone. The place still holds on to the old world charm with the same simplistic decor and bench-style seating arrangements where great Bengalis from novelists to freedom fighters have enjoyed their 'sherbets'. You will find the list of all such famous Bengalis along with some of their pictures.
Their famous 'daaber sherbet' is ideal during summer months as a thirst quencher. I have tried their mango 'lassi' but did not quite like it. I felt the yoghurt was not thick enough and diluted with a lot of ice.
But, I am absolutely in love with the Passion Fruit sherbet and you just keep guessing as the different fruit flavors hit you. It contains wood apple (bael), mango, and many other fruits. It is a must try if you happen to drop by in College Street, especially on a hot afternoon.

When you enter you would come to know this place is standing there in pride since the inception of Kolkata, it has seen history being made. You will find paper cuts of reviews, a board shows who were the legendary visitors who stepped in here, and of course in another board you find the menu.
You would be offered a seat in their retro style wooden tables and chairs, and then you place the order, Grape Crush, Dub Sarbet, Green Mango, Tamarinds, Kesar Malai are the drinks I am a little biased towards, out of which Dub and Tamarind are my all time favourite. 
A glass of any of the drinks will leave you completely refreshed and ready to hop around the book stores again. 
I am seriously in love with this place. Good Bless them a 100 years of more life.

A little problem, they remain closed for around 3-4 months during the winter, considering that people are reluctant to have cold drinks at that period of time. I wonder !!!!

Recommended.

2014-05-15 18:38:38
Somrita Chandra
2404624
4.5
Paramount..the name itself is a signature in bengali food n beverage industry. ....possesses a rich taste of bengal and praised by almost every eminent personality (Starting from freedom fighters to scientists, novelists/writers to directors/actors,sportsperso s n all)
Now, it comes to their spread...they have three types of variants in sherbets-
 1) Syrup based 
 2) Malai based
 3) Cream or curd based
In syrup ranges,I have tried their green mango and litchi, which I liked.
In malai based they have strawberry n coco malai..have tasted strawberry (am nt so very fond of coco or chocolate flavour) n it was heavenly.It is garnished with kaju n kishmish...:)
In curd based, have tried green mango, vanilla, pineapple n orange...they r delicious. 
But itz their signature sherbe twhich is my hot favourite-Daab sherbet..an awesome concoction with daaber sansh (the soft kernel of green coconut) & daaber jol...it is the showstopper.
All d sherbets r served with crushed ice, w/t ice, they charge 2 bucks extra for every glass.
Ambiance:-
This hadn't changed their original interior, still very much retained their old calcutta charm.A non ac joint, but the time their sherbets arrive, u'll forget all d heat!! A place where one can come with friends, family or all alone!!
The staffs are courteous n will help you gladly
If u r in a fix to choose one... 
They can accommodate arnd 25 people at a time, due to space crunch...so in puja times one has to wait long..so deducted 0.5 for that.
Overall rating :4.5/5
P.S.:one can takaway his /her fav sherbet, they have that facilty!!

Almost a century old, still holding the flag of one of the must visit destinations of foodies in Kolkata and no competition. 
I hope the decoration of this place will remain same even after another century, because it is one of very few beverage shop where you can forget current date and imagine yourself having sip of "coco-malai" in the summer of 1961 or before than that, yes it is such a nostalgic place. Generation after generation have been visiting this place and quenching thirst with Dab-Sarbat, Keshar Malai, Passion fruits etc.
My favorite from the list is "Passion-fruit rubry base", the same taste and the flavor can not be found anywhere else. I think The malai items(Keshar, Banana, Rose,Strawberry etc.) and Dab-sarbats can be prepared in home but "Passion-fruit rubry base" does have special ingredients which give it distinct taste,texture and flavor. My instinct they use Bel-fruit in it. Do visit this place and give a try with "Passion-fruit rubry base".

##

2014-02-06 22:57:38
Subhayan Chakraborty
600058
4.0
As far as my knowledge permits, this juice shop is probably the first of its kind in the city. It's also reached a level of fame that has made it a part of the culinary traditions of north kolkata.

Located on the road bordering the back side of college square ( if you consider the College street side as front ), it has a small seating area with bare ambience. The menu is limited with a clear division between the specialized drinks which are clearly overpriced and the ordinary drinks such as the rose, pineapple, grape, strawberry syrups.
I felt that the price is extremely unreasonable across the board. Having said that, the drinks are superb. We had the Dub Sherbat which is one of their more famous items. Its a tall glass of coconut milk mixed with a generous proportion of the kernel and ice blocks. The taste is one of unadulterated purity. I suspect that they also add a carefully balanced sweet solution but that's a trade secret. :)

Chakraborty Tip : I'm not a particular fan of the many specialised juice and mocktail bars in the city, primarily because they are not standalone establishments. It's extremely awkward to enter a 4 star hotel in order to grab a glass of sherbet. In that regard, this place is a must try.

##

2014-02-01 14:16:26
Anuj.juna
65284
4.5
Easily on the "do not miss" list of places to eat/drink in Calcutta. This tiny, freshly painted and immaculately maintained place serves some of the most interest drinks in town.

You can start with the Dab (coconut) sherbet (Rs 40, Jan 2014) or get right to it with the Choco Malai (Rs 80) which is this delicious chocolately concoction topped with fresh malai (cream) and dry fruits. Or you could go with the slightly intoxicating Grape Crush. 

You sit on long benches and all sherbets are served in tall glasses with spoons so you can cull out the pieces of coconut meat (in the Dab Sherbet) or the malai (in the choco malai) or the grapes (Grape crush). If you are lucky, you can meet the owner and hear stories of how this place used to be a meeting hole for the revolutionaries in the Independence movement.

Delightful place.

2014-01-29 14:46:15
Dev Reinstated
398498
5.0
Writing about this place is like a Nostalgia for me... My Presidency days and our little sneak out from college class timings...

Paramount has been synonymous to a rich legacy itself. The sherbets here, are a cult and has been delivering quality for decades now. From celebrities to commoners, Calcuttans have sweared by Paramount. The curd based drink is like heavens from the unbearable heat of the city. Found in various flavors, ranging from Rose to Mango, from Banana to Kesar; these sherbets have never failed to delight us with their taste and aroma.

My personal fav are the Dab Malai (Coconut) which they serve with pieces of semi-formed coconut chunks. The Coco Malai is one more hot fav, where they blend the distinctive tastes of coco and cream together. the space is less and it is not air-conditioned, but these factors don't stand a chance against their offering. Superlatively reasonable prices make it a attraction itself. 

So on a whole, its a small trip to heaven itself.

You can even fly down from a different city for this :P
